# Yex Technical Document Section 0

## Overview of 1caf22
This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 0.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 1caf22_0

### API Reference: Method_1
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 1ms latency.

This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 1150.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 545378_1150

### API Reference: Method_1151
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 1151ms latency.

This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 2134.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 4e10f2_2134

### API Reference: Method_2135
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 2135ms latency.

This deep-dive analysis covers the symbolic execution of Yex nodes at layer 2274.

### Optimization Strategy
- Node Flattening
- AST Pruning
- Memory Recycling

Build ID: 228cc6_2274

### API Reference: Method_2275
Accepts a `YexNode` and returns a `Future<Structure>`. Highly performant at 2275ms latency.
